<response>None</response>< Text>
Was hoping for so much more especially for the location. The restaurant is fairly small. We were 1 of maybe 3 tables being occupied at the time. There was one server. We went during lunch time. I placed my order with the server which she repeated to me incorrectly. I corrected her. Several minutes later she returned to confirm our orders having us realize the kitchen hadn't even started firing it up yet. She once again tried to confirm an incorrect order. She was corrected again, twice, because I was getting worried. When our food arrived it was completely wrong and exactly how she had been erroneously trying to confirm prior. She told me just to eat around what I didn't order and a separate plate was brought out with the correct sides. I ordered an iced tea and was told there was not enough left. She had stated she would bring their pozole soup for my daughter but never did and had to be reminded when the food arrived. The food was bland and there was a spice, perhaps cinnamon or nutmeg, that was very overwhelming. Such a disappointing experience. We will not return and do not expect for it to last long in Carmel if experiences like ours are the norm. Price for 2 item combo was close to $20 per plate. The positive, rice was decent and cooked well.</Text>

<Time>1561698159700</Time>< Rating>

<Review>Wow. I usually don't leave bad reviews instead I just don't review it. If you don't have anything nice to say, say nothing. But I am making an exception to this place. I don't know were the high star reviews came from. We were looking for a place to eat after a morning at the beach with the family, and saw the high star reviews and decided to try it. It was a very bad experience. Despite there being only two tables of less than three people and us a party of six with three front house people everything took forever. While we waited to order after having asked for drinks, two other tables came in and left after minutes of just sitting. First red flag. There was a couple sitting next to us that appeared to have finished their queso fundido long ago, when their food arrived. The gentleman just had a bite of his beef tacos and stopped eating, although his companion just stuck to finishing the plate quickly - we at the time assumed he didn't have a big appetite. Second red flag. By this time we had waited 10 minutes to order after having gotten our aguas frescas. The menu items looked promising albeit pricey for common Mexican food -not high dinning. As soon as we ordered the couple next to us asked for their check, it took 15 minutes for the check to arrive, by then we knew we had made a mistake to stick around. We waited 45 for our food and even asked since the other table had just recieved theirs. As soon as we asked about the delay our food started to come in person by person. First dish on the table were the chicken taquitos. The chicken mole taquitos were cold, the sauce watery, and the chicken in them barely had any mole we even asked what had happened to the mole -in their defense they brought us a side of mole. Minutes later, the Guadalajara tacos  made their appearance on the table. The meat was over cooked and didn't taste like Mexican seasoning, although the presentation was great and portions were a decent size. However, the biggest faux paus was that the tortillas for the tacos took minutes to arrive so rice and beans were eaten first. We had asked for three orders of tacos  but only got tortillas for two orders so one person had to wait extra time. When we asked about the whereabouts of the third order we were told they were out. And we had to wait for more to be made. Lastly the mole came in, which was watery and tasted store bought only enhanced with a stick of cinnamon in the process. The meal was overpriced for the quality and time we waited, around 20 dollars per plate. I have had better tasting, authentic, and faster Mexican food out of food trucks in Oakland or San Francisco for half the price. During the entire time we never got asked for a refill on our drinks and we dared not asked for fear of waiting 15 minutes for it. I am a person who has been around the restaurant business for decades, and do not mind the wait or price if service and food are of quality. However, this place didn't have the service or quality. The only thing I can say is that the presentation of some of their plates is great, and their tortillas are hand made and good quality. As we were leaving the lady who makes the tortillas set up shop and was making the tortillas to the public by the window. It was cool to see that and that is why I give them a star.<//Review><Pics>None</Pics>< resp>

Our visit here for Valentine's Day was perfect! This place looks like it came straight from 17th Century France but the interior is new and incredibly clean. The staff was awesome and kind -- the food was great, and I found that we derived a lot of value for what we paid. I plan to come back here every few months during COVID as a nice getaway from home. Highly recommend this charming place!<//Text>

<Response>None<//Response><Pics>None< /Pics><Text>Enchante is my new go-to romantic getaway hotel!  I've stayed there twice now, and I have to say that their fantastic staff is matched by a truly charming and comfortable facility.  We are welcomed with a smile any time of day or night (along with our pets, whom they have considered as well).  Each room at Enchante is themed: Apothique, Marie Antoinette, and Amerique are a few.  Guests are treated to a complimentary charcuterie plate in the evening, and a breakfast each morning.  When I made a booking error, the staff bent over backwards to accommodate me for an additional night... for which I will be eternally grateful!

Whether you're in town for business or just a vacation in the South Bay/South Peninsula, Enchante is a worthy choice.  Downtown Los Altos is just steps away, with so many choices for food and entertainment that you would never need to stray far.  Cupertino is home to one of the largest Taiwanese communities outside Taiwan so it's an excellent base camp if you're looking for a weekend of comfort food.

Parking can be tricky on busy weekends, and the occasional Street Festival blocks off the road - so be sure to check with the hotel before parking your car for the night.< /Text>< name>

< text>
This is my favorite Starbucks because it use to be a burger king and when I was a kid our school bus would actually take us here for some unexplained reason, this sealing a love for the King and his burgers. Fast forward a decade and there I was as a young adult and it had become a cheesesteak shop, the sandwiches were delicious but the big secret was the amazing Mexican food the nice older gals in back would wip up if you knew how to ask, yet it went out of business, dark times indeed.

Skip forward another few years and this guy Bill who while super nice was clearly on some sorta drugs you would buy at a party in sun valley stole the menu from T's Rotisserie in a incline village. This was hilarious to me because the recipies were actually from the family of a man named Sergio whom Bill was also able to steal from T's. I dont know this T person but they were probably upset at this whole situation. Anyway they gave away free food their first day open and I ate 8 burritos. Swear to God, EIGHT over a 10 hour period. We had been lifted from the dark times of no great food next to the mousehole. After what seems like 5 years those party drugs seemed to have done their job and the thousand yard stares from the Bill's Rotisserie senior employees had gotten too consistent. Their talented chef left and opened Golden Rotisserie a few blocks away and sealed this weird buildings fate to be empty again. It was empty and grossly neglected looking for a while. Picture homeless meth heads and bears staying away. Imagine how that feels to see a childhood friend who became a lifelong presence existing like this.

Finally, Starbucks, came to the rescue and remodeled this place into what's now a rather nice location. I was able to convince a girl to move here from another state for this location and my dog so you will have a hard time convincing me it's not the best, highest rated Starbucks in the world, actually. Halle is my favorite barista, she makes the chocolate milk with half coconut milk and it will blow your mind.

A lot of cops hang out here, I dont have a problem with this but you might, man.

Fyi, I dont even like Starbucks or coffee in general so I would imagine if you got this far into my review and are into coffee you will be well served by visiting.</text>

Was excited to try this place, the drinks looked great on the website and the patio looked cute when walking down locust. So we decided to give it a try.

We ordered two drinks, a pour of tremana reposado tequila and a margarita. We wanted to order the mole for dinner but they were out. So we ordered some tacos. < Date>
1487970579948</Date>
<rate>5<//rate>< review>
Parked here for a short trip to Cabo. Indoor parking, shuttle right to airport, good experience going to airport. When we came back a few days later we got right on the Wallypark shuttle, the driver was friendly and took us right to our car, dropped us off and left with the other passengers. To our surprise, apparently we left an inside light on in our car for the 5 days we were gone so the battery was dead as a door nail. I was thinking oh boy, now I get to call AAA and it will be 30 minutes at least before they would be there. At that time the shuttle driver was going back by, we asked if he had jumper cables, he said no but they have a portable booster and he would get someone to assist us. Within 5 minutes a nice young lady came walking up with a jumper box, hooked it all up and we were able to start our car. What could have been a real pain, turned out to be a great experience. Heck, they even offered us bottles of water on the way out. Nothing but good to say about Wallypark SD and all the employees we dealt with. Thank you.<//review>

< review>
First off, Crescent City is the most beautiful little town on the coast that you could find. While on a business trip I always stop by this McDonald's for breakfast and they are always busy. With that said, just because they are busy does not mean that they lack in customer service in expediting orders and getting people in and out as quickly as possible never rushing anyone. I've had nothing but great experiences going there. My food is always hot, my order is always accurate and the the ladies and gentleman at the front front counter always have a smile and a warm welcome waiting for me. I know this is hard work so I really appreciate the fact that I can go in and be treated like I'm a neighbor or a friend and still get a great dining experience. This cannot be said about all McDonald's which is why this one is so rare. I hope that one day everybody gets a chance to have a dining experience such as I have had at this McDonald's in Crescent City every time I go. Thanks again you guys the team McDonald's Crescent City rocks!< /review>
